rating:4.5
posted:Posted March 17, 2024
msg:The main building of the hotel is a typical Hui-style building, very beautiful. In addition, there are single-family houses, townhouses, and a large lake view garden with a beautiful and quiet environment. It is only a 15-minute walk from the Kecun Visitor Center. Because there are many guests who come to worship Buddha, the breakfast buffet also has a vegetarian area, which is very considerate. Secondly, I feel that the hotel treats Ctrip guests preferentially. When we were having breakfast, the receptionist saw that the color of our ticket was different from others, so he called us and brought us yogurt from the bar. A fruit plate was also given when we checked in. But I feel that the hotel seems to have cut costs too much: the marble floor of the bathroom and the marble countertop of the bathtub are stained (see photos), and it is estimated that it cannot be cleaned by ordinary cleaning; there are no umbrellas, scales (which I just use), and refrigerators; not everyone has yogurt for breakfast...

name:2â€0â€0â€9â€1â€0â€6â€6â€1â€6
info:Deluxe Twin Room with Lake View
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:6 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 17, 2024
msg:The hotel is located about seven or eight minutes away from the No. 4 gate of Dayuan Cultural Park. The environment is good. It is a typical Su-Anhui horse head wall style building. The front desk ladies are very enthusiastic and the service is very professional. The room is well-equipped and there is a fruit plate for check-in.
In the hotel's vast garden, you can see the 99-meter-high Buddha from afar. The gardens with small bridges, pavilions and towers are full of birdsong and flowers, which makes people feel relaxed and happy.
There are many hotels around, which is very convenient for travel.
The only drawback is that the sound insulation of the corridor is slightly poor, and the sound of closing the door of the next room is a bit noisy.
